              // Print form to set bring focus/new window cookie
              // (c)2001 James "furn" Furness <furn@base6.com>

              function SetCookie (name, value, days) {
                  // set expiry date to 'days' from now.
                  var expires = new Date();
                  expires.setTime(expires.getTime() + (days * 24 * 3600 * 1000));

                  document.cookie = name + "=" + escape(value) +
                                    "; expires=" + expires.toGMTString() +
                                    "; domain=bluesnews.com; path=/";
              }

              function GetCookie (name) {
                  var arg = name + "=";
                  var alen = arg.length;
                  var clen = document.cookie.length;
                  var i = 0;

                  while (i < clen) {
                      var j = i + alen;

                      if (document.cookie.substring(i, j) == arg)
                          return getCookieVal(j);

                      i = document.cookie.indexOf(" ", i) + 1;
                      if (i == 0)
                          break;
                  }

                  return null;
              }

              function updateTargetCookieT (obj) {
                  if (obj.checked) {
                      SetCookie("settarget", "true", 365);
                  } else {
                      SetCookie("settarget", "false", 365);
                  }
                  location.reload();
              }

              var settarget = GetCookie("settarget");

              document.write('<FORM><INPUT TYPE="checkbox" onClick="updateTargetCookieT(this)"' + (settarget == "true" ? ' CHECKED' : '') + '> Launch Links<' + '/FORM>');

      <table cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" border="0"><tr valign="bottom"><td><h2 class="posting"><a href="/s/132041/ridge-racer-unbounded-demo" target="_self">Ridge Racer Unbounded Demo</a></h2></td><td><h2 class="postdate">  [10:11 am ET] - <a href="/s/132041/ridge-racer-unbounded-demo" target="_self">Share</a> - <a href="/cgi-bin/board.pl?action=viewthread&amp;boardid=1&amp;threadid=132041" target="_self">13 Comments</a></h2></td></tr></table>
      <div class="posting">
The <a href="http://store.steampowered.com/app/202310/"><b>Ridge Racer Unbounded</b> Page on Steam</a> now offers a playable demo for the latest installment in the Ridge Racer series of racing simulations. We have no details on the demo itself, but here's a brief overview of the game: &quot;RIDGE RACER Unbounded brings an unexpected dimension to the series, delivering an original blast of ferocious racing adrenaline. Join the Unbounded street racing gang, lead by Kara Shindo, and test your driving skills against rivals in every street and alley of Shatter Bay. Prove your worth, get respect and expand your turf.&quot; Thanks Frans.
      <p></p>
      </div>      <table cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" border="0"><tr valign="bottom"><td><h2 class="posting"><a href="/s/132040/last-stronghold-3-patch-next-week" target="_self">Last Stronghold 3 Patch Next Week</a></h2></td><td><h2 class="postdate">  [10:08 am ET] - <a href="/s/132040/last-stronghold-3-patch-next-week" target="_self">Share</a> - <a href="/cgi-bin/board.pl?action=viewthread&amp;boardid=1&amp;threadid=132040" target="_self">6 Comments</a></h2></td></tr></table>
      <div class="posting">
Firefly Studios announces plans to release a new patch for <b>Stronghold 3</b> a week from today, saying the version 1.10 patch is their last planned update for the strategy sequel. Then new version will include a bunch of user-requested changes and a new &quot;Coronation&quot; multiplayer mode. Here's word: <blockquote><p><font face="Arial, Helvetica" size="2" color="#FFFF80">In Coronation Mode players will race to become the King of Kings. Players start off at the lowly rank of “Village Idiot” with limited access to buildings and military units. By generating honour players can move up the ranks, gaining new technology and weaponry along the way. For the first time in a Stronghold game Coronation mode also features upgradable keeps, which have their own defences and provide additional housing for workers and troops. The first King to achieve the rank of “Emperor” will win the game and can rightly claim to be the ultimate Stronghold Lord.<br>
</font></p></blockquote> <i><a target="_self" href="/s/132040/last-stronghold-3-patch-next-week">Continue here</a> to read the full story</i>.
      <p></p>
      </div>      <table cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" border="0"><tr valign="bottom"><td><h2 class="posting"><a href="/s/132039/blood-bowl-chaos-edition-announced" target="_self">Blood Bowl: Chaos Edition Announced</a></h2></td><td><h2 class="postdate">  [09:58 am ET] - <a href="/s/132039/blood-bowl-chaos-edition-announced" target="_self">Share</a> - <a href="/cgi-bin/board.pl?action=viewthread&amp;boardid=1&amp;threadid=132039" target="_self">14 Comments</a></h2></td></tr></table>
      <div class="posting">
The <a href="http://www.bloodbowl-game.com/index.php?rub=news-info&id=300">Blood Bowl Website</a> announces <b>Blood Bowl: Chaos Edition</b>, an updated edition of their Warhammer meets tackle football mash-up expected this September. The new edition will add three new races, a new stadium, and a new World Championship mode, though it's not stated if this is an expansion or a new product, but as we wait for more details, they offer some screenshots in the meantime, and here's a bit on what's new: &quot;World Championship mode expands even further the solo experience of Blood Bowl. From national qualifying games to continental cups to the final tournament, the competition just got bloodier! The online mode will of course be available with its intense matches, vicious private leagues, and global rankings! Get ready for another round of high fantasy football as Blood Bowl: Chaos Edition races for the touchdown!&quot;

      <table cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" border="0"><tr valign="bottom"><td><h2 class="posting"><a href="/s/132029/saints-row-3-standalone-expansion-plans" target="_self">Saints Row 3 Standalone Expansion Plans</a></h2></td><td><h2 class="postdate">  [8:24 pm ET] - <a href="/s/132029/saints-row-3-standalone-expansion-plans" target="_self">Share</a> - <a href="/cgi-bin/board.pl?action=viewthread&amp;boardid=1&amp;threadid=132029" target="_self">33 Comments</a></h2></td></tr></table>
      <div class="posting">
<a href="http://www.thq.com/uk/sr3-enter-the-dominatrix/go/article/view/homepage_article/257951/saints_row®:_the_third™_–_enter_the_dominatrix™_announced">THQ announces</a> Saints Row The Third: Enter The Dominatrix, a standalone expansion coming this fall for Volition's open world action sequel. Saying this is &quot;no longer an April Fool's dream,&quot; they promise &quot;the most requested gameplay features from the Saints Row community: freaking super powers.&quot; Here's a bit:<blockquote><p><font face="Arial, Helvetica" size="2" color="#FFFF80">Enter the Dominatrix picks up immediately following the events of Saints Row: The Third. For centuries, alien warlord Zinyak has eyed Earth and its precious natural resources and females with a watchful eye. As he prepares an armada for invasion, he has only one worry: the Third Street Saints.<br>
<br>
Once a simple street gang from Stilwater, the Saints have evolved into a global empire, replete with bombastic TV advertising and tasteful consumer products, the kind of TV advertising and consumer products that would give any alien warlord pause. Clearly, the Saints are the biggest badasses on Earth.<br>
<br>
Now, in order to prepare his forces for domination, Zinyak captures the leader of the Saints and imprisons him in an elaborate virtual reality simulation. This simulation program looks and feels like Steelport, but it is the world that has been pulled over your eyes to blind you from the truth. Here, you are a slave. Welcome... to the Dominatrix.<br>
<br>
More details and a first look at Saints Row: The Third – Enter the Dominatrix will be available this summer. Make sure you're following Saints Row on <a href="http://www.twitter.com/saintsrow">Twitter</a> and <a href="http://www.facebook.com/saintsrow">Facebook</a> to stay up to date with the latest.</font></p></blockquote>
      <p></p>
      </div>      <table cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" border="0"><tr valign="bottom"><td><h2 class="posting"><a href="/s/132028/official-the-elder-scrolls-online-announcement" target="_self">Official The Elder Scrolls Online Announcement</a></h2></td><td><h2 class="postdate">  [8:24 pm ET] - <a href="/s/132028/official-the-elder-scrolls-online-announcement" target="_self">Share</a> - <a href="/cgi-bin/board.pl?action=viewthread&amp;boardid=1&amp;threadid=132028" target="_self">42 Comments</a></h2></td></tr></table>
      <div class="posting">
<a href="http://www.marketwatch.com/story/bethesda-softworks-announces-the-elder-scrolls-online-2012-05-03">This press release</a> officially announces <b>The Elder Scrolls Online</b>, the <a target="_self" href="/s/132013/the-elder-scrolls-online-next-year">just-revealed</a> MMOG. The announcement offers a bit more on the game:<blockquote><p><font face="Arial, Helvetica" size="2" color="#FFFF80">Bethesda Softworks®, a ZeniMax® Media company, today announced The Elder Scrolls® Online, an MMO in development at ZeniMax Online Studios. The Elder Scrolls Online will be the first Elder Scrolls game to allow gamers to explore the legendary Elder Scrolls world with others.<br>
<br>
The Elder Scrolls Online is being developed for PC and Mac under the leadership of industry veteran Matt Firor, who has spent the last two decades working in online game development. Details about the game are revealed in an exclusive cover story in Game Informer®'s June issue, which ships to subscribers and newsstands this month.<br>
<br>
&quot;We have been working hard to create an online world in which players will be able to experience the epic Elder Scrolls universe with their friends, something fans have long said they wanted,&quot; said Matt Firor, game director of The Elder Scrolls Online. &quot;It will be extremely rewarding finally to unveil what we have been developing the last several years. The entire team is committed to creating the best MMO ever made - and one that is worthy of The Elder Scrolls franchise.&quot;</font></p></blockquote>
      <p></p>
      </div>      <table cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" border="0"><tr valign="bottom"><td><h2 class="posting"><a href="/s/132027/sanctum-collection-free-weekend-free-dlc" target="_self">Sanctum Collection; Free Weekend; Free DLC</a></h2></td><td><h2 class="postdate">  [8:23 pm ET] - <a href="/s/132027/sanctum-collection-free-weekend-free-dlc" target="_self">Share</a> - <a href="/cgi-bin/board.pl?action=viewthread&amp;boardid=1&amp;threadid=132027" target="_self">Post a Comment</a></h2></td></tr></table>

Both the <a href="http://store.steampowered.com/sub/12184/">Collection</a> and the original <a href="http://store.steampowered.com/app/91600/">Sanctum</a> are on sale on Steam for 75% off, and the game <a href="http://store.steampowered.com/news/7889/">can be played for free this weekend</a> on <a href="http://www.steampowered.com/">Steam</a>. If all that's not enough, there is also a new <a href="http://store.steampowered.com/app/91609/">free Yogscave DLC on Steam</a> as well as a <a href="http://store.steampowered.com/news/7882/">new automatic patch for the game</a>. Here are the highlights of the new version:</p>
<ul>
	<li>Brand New Medal System</li>
	<li>Improved Balancing</li>
	<li>Graphic Details Settings</li>
	<li>Under the Hood Tweaks</li>
</ul>

      </div>      <table cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" border="0"><tr valign="bottom"><td><h2 class="posting"><a href="/s/132026/the-may-hurray-bundle" target="_self">The May Hurray Bundle</a></h2></td><td><h2 class="postdate">  [8:23 pm ET] - <a href="/s/132026/the-may-hurray-bundle" target="_self">Share</a> - <a href="/cgi-bin/board.pl?action=viewthread&amp;boardid=1&amp;threadid=132026" target="_self">8 Comments</a></h2></td></tr></table>
      <div class="posting">
The <a href="http://www.indieroyale.com/">Indie Royale Website</a> now offers The May Hurray Bundle an new collection of five independent games offered at a &quot;bargain, fluctuating price.&quot; This includes <b>Dungeon Defenders</b>, <b>Containment: The Zombie Puzzler</b>, <b>Data Jammers: FastForward</b>, <b>Brainpipe - A Plunge to Unhumanity</b>, and <b>Weird Worlds: Return to Infinite Space</b>.       </div>      <table cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" border="0"><tr valign="bottom"><td><h2 class="posting"><a href="/s/132025/mass-effect-3-connection-issues" target="_self">Mass Effect 3 Connection Issues</a></h2></td><td><h2 class="postdate">  [8:23 pm ET] - <a href="/s/132025/mass-effect-3-connection-issues" target="_self">Share</a> - <a href="/cgi-bin/board.pl?action=viewthread&amp;boardid=1&amp;threadid=132025" target="_self">17 Comments</a></h2></td></tr></table>
      <div class="posting">
<a href="http://social.bioware.com/forum/1/topic/344/index/11821829">This post</a> and <a href="http://social.bioware.com/forum/1/topic/343/index/11828744/1">this one</a> on the BioWare Social Network have complaints from players encountering errors when attempting to play <b>Mass Effect 3</b> multiplayer. Most of this seems to involve being told they require an &quot;online pass,&quot; which does not exist for the PC version of the game, as it is used as a way of combating used console game sales. There are also indications that those who own the From Ashes DLC are not even able to play the game in singleplayer mode. There are posts from players claiming they've been told BioWare is working on the problem. Thanks Mark.

Company of heroes to is expected to arrives [sic] in 2013.&quot; Company of Heroes Online, the MMO installment in the series closed <a target="_self" href="/s/120134/company-of-heroes-patched-company-of-heroes-online-ending">over a year ago</a>, and rumors of CoH2 first surfaced <a target="_self" href="/s/128576/company-of-heroes-2">late last year</a>.

      </div>      <table cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" border="0"><tr valign="bottom"><td><h2 class="posting"><a href="/s/132013/the-elder-scrolls-online-next-year" target="_self">The Elder Scrolls Online Next Year</a></h2></td><td><h2 class="postdate">  [12:37 pm ET] - <a href="/s/132013/the-elder-scrolls-online-next-year" target="_self">Share</a> - <a href="/cgi-bin/board.pl?action=viewthread&amp;boardid=1&amp;threadid=132013" target="_self">86 Comments</a></h2></td></tr></table>
      <div class="posting">
<a href="http://www.gameinformer.com/b/features/archive/2012/05/03/june-cover-revealed-the-elder-scrolls-online.aspx">Game Informer's June 2012 Cover Reveal</a> shows the next issue of the magazine will offer the official unveiling of <b>The Elder Scrolls Online</b>, finally fulfilling long-time speculation that Bethesda would one day create an MMO based on their popular RPG series. They say the game will come to Windows and OS X next year, and that a teaser trailer a screenshot will be posted tomorrow. Here's what they reveal so far:<blockquote><p><font face="Arial, Helvetica" size="2" color="#FFFF80">Developed by the team at Zenimax Online Studios, The Elder Scrolls Online merges the unmatched exploration of rich worlds that the franchise is known for with the scale and social aspects of a massively multiplayer online role-playing game. Players will discover an entirely new chapter of Elder Scrolls history in this ambitious world, set a millennium before the events of Skyrim as the daedric prince Molag Bal tries to pull all of Tamriel into his demonic realm.<br>
<br>
&quot;It will be extremely rewarding finally to unveil what we have been developing the last several years,&quot; said game director and MMO veteran Matt Firor, whose previous work includes Mythic's well-received Dark Age of Camelot. &quot;The entire team is committed to creating the best MMO ever made – and one that is worthy of The Elder Scrolls franchise.&quot;<br>
<br>
An in-depth look at everything from solo questing to public dungeons awaits in our enormous June cover story – as well as a peek at the player-driven PvP conflict that pits the three player factions against each other in open-world warfare over the province of Cyrodiil and the Emperor's throne itself.</font></p></blockquote>

<a href="http://www.isotx.com/?p=3836">ISOTX Website</a> announces the new <b>Scorched Earth</b> DLC pack for <b>Iron Grip: Warlord</b> is now live <a href="http://store.steampowered.com/app/31713/">on Steam</a>, offering new content for this first-person shooter/tower defense hybrid. The announcement doesn't offer any details on the DLC, <a href="http://www.isotx.com/?p=3588">but this earlier post</a> offers a video, images, and information. ISOTX does take the occasion to outline how you can attempt to snag a free copy of the DLC by participating in a giveaway program. With <a href="http://tera-europe.com/newsdetail/article/the-launch-of-tera-in-europe.html">today's launch</a> of <a href="http://tera-europe.com/home.html"><b>TERA</b> in Europe</a> joining <a href="http://tera.enmasse.com/">TERA North America</a>, both editions of Bluehole Studios' MMORPG are live. Not following the rush to free-to-play, TERA requires both the purchase of the retail game along with monthly subscription. Here's a thumbnail of the game: &quot;New players will begin their adventure in TERA by creating a highly customised character from seven races and eight classes. They will join forces with thousands of allies to save an endangered universe. They will vie for power and set their own rules through an advanced political system. TERA players will discover a one-of-a-kind experience, giving them an MMO game setting combined with the thrill of action games.&quot;

      <div class="posting">
Though we don't see an announcements anywhere referring to this, there is now a red banner across the top of the front page of <a href="http://www.fileplanet.com/">FilePlanet</a> from indicating that this files archive is no longer active, saying: &quot;Note: FilePlanet is no longer being updated and is in the process of being archived.&quot; This game file repository that was once popular enough to successfully charge subscription fees was launched by GameSpy back in the late 20th century. It came into the possession of IGN in 2004 and a year later IGN was acquired by Rupert Murdoch's News Corp. Thanks Auger.

      </div>      <table cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" border="0"><tr valign="bottom"><td><h2 class="posting"><a href="/s/132007/renaissance-heroes-announced" target="_self">Renaissance Heroes Announced</a></h2></td><td><h2 class="postdate">  [09:37 am ET] - <a href="/s/132007/renaissance-heroes-announced" target="_self">Share</a> - <a href="/cgi-bin/board.pl?action=viewthread&amp;boardid=1&amp;threadid=132007" target="_self">4 Comments</a></h2></td></tr></table>
      <div class="posting">
ChangYou.com (US) announces Renaissance Heroes as the new name for a project previously known as &quot;DaVinci Online.&quot; This upcoming multiplayer first-person shooter is set in 16th century Renaissance Europe, which was apparently home to more gunfights than we were previous aware. The <a href="http://www.renaissanceheroes.com/">Renaissance Heroes Website</a> has <a href="http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=5dDj7ZTccNo">a trailer</a>, art, information, and is accepting signups for the game's upcoming closed beta test. Here's word: &quot;The game, previously known as &quot;DaVinci Online,&quot; combines classic multiplayer action with unparalleled visual realism powered by the Unreal Engine 3 technology to deliver the fun of fast-action shooters to a new generation of gamers. Renaissance Heroes invites players of all skill levels to experience the adrenaline-pumping action coupled with easy accessibility in a completely free to play environment later this year.&quot;

      <div class="posting">
<a href="https://twitter.com/#!/notch">Markus Persson's Twitter</a> has strong reactions from Mojang's Markus 'Notch' Persson to the oddity of the <a href="http://store.steampowered.com/sub/14499/">EA Indie Bundle on Steam</a>, as it would be a stretch to refer to anything related to the giant Electronic Arts as &quot;indie&quot; (in the same stretch of tweets he objects to even calling Mojang an &quot;indie&quot;). Beginning <a href="https://twitter.com/#!/notch/status/197991770817167360">by saying</a>: &quot;EA releases an 'indie bundle'? That's not how that works, EA. Stop attempting to ruin everything, you bunch of cynical bastards,&quot; he <a href="https://twitter.com/#!/notch/status/197992550144032768">follows with</a> &quot;Indies are saving gaming. EA is methodically destroying it.&quot; He <a href="https://twitter.com/#!/notch/status/198013445726142464">caps this off</a> with a clarification of what he's faulting here: &quot;I got into trouble on the interwebs again! The games in the bundle are good, I'm not questioning them. I'm questioning EA.&quot; Thanks <a href="http://www.develop-online.net/news/40685/Notch-EA-methodically-destroying-gaming">Develop</a>.

      </div>      <table cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" border="0"><tr valign="bottom"><td><h2 class="posting"><a href="/s/131996/out-of-the-blue" target="_self">Out of the Blue</a></h2></td><td><h2 class="postdate">  [09:36 am ET] - <a href="/s/131996/out-of-the-blue" target="_self">Share</a> - <a href="/cgi-bin/board.pl?action=viewthread&amp;boardid=1&amp;threadid=131996" target="_self">16 Comments</a></h2></td></tr></table>
      <div class="posting">
I assume the rain overnight around here was accompanied by lightning and thunder. I didn't hear anything, but Hudson the wonder dog woke me up having one of her panic attacks that are triggered by such noises. I did my best to comfort her, and looked at the situation as another argument in favor of MrsBlue and I accepting the offer to relocate to L.A., as they rarely suffer the kind of storms that have become the norm all summer in these parts, and I'm pretty convinced her getting so freaked out by such things is shortening her lifespan.</p>

function getCookieVal (offset) {
   var endstr = document.cookie.indexOf (";", offset);

   if (endstr == -1)
      endstr = document.cookie.length;

   return unescape(document.cookie.substring(offset, endstr));
}

function SetTargetCookie (name, value) {
   // set expiry date to 1 year from now.
   var expires = new Date ();
   expires.setTime(expires.getTime() + (30 * 24 * 3600 * 1000));

   document.cookie = name + "=" + escape (value) +
                     "; expires=" + expires.toGMTString();
}

function updateTargetCookieT (obj) {
   if (obj.checked) {
      SetCookie("settarget", "true");
   } else {
      SetCookie("settarget", "false");
   }
   location.reload();
}

function updateTargetCookie (obj) {
   if (obj.checked) {
      SetTargetCookie("bbgclr", "true");
   } else {
      SetTargetCookie("bbgclr", "false");
   }
   location.reload();
}

function GetCookie (name) {
   var arg = name + "=";
   var alen = arg.length;
   var clen = document.cookie.length;
   var i = 0;

   while (i < clen) {
      var j = i + alen;

      if (document.cookie.substring(i, j) == arg)
         return getCookieVal (j);

      i = document.cookie.indexOf(" ", i) + 1;
      if (i == 0)
         break;
   }

   return null;
}


// Logo launch code by Jason "loonyboi" Bergman and his team of infinite monkeys
function launchlogo() {
   logoinfo = window.open('/popup.shtml','logoinfo','toolbar=no,location=no,directories=no,status=no,menubar=no,scrollbars=no,resizable=no,width=360,height=350,left=50,top=50');
}

var settarget = GetCookie('settarget');

if (settarget == "true") {
   document.write('<base target="_blank">');
} else {
   document.write('<base target="_top">');
}

function setActiveStyleSheet(title) {

  if (DOMok() == true) {
    var i, a;
    for (i=0; (a = document.getElementsByTagName("link")[i]); i++) {
      if (a.getAttribute("rel").indexOf("style") != -1 &&
          a.getAttribute("title")) {
        a.disabled = true;
        if (a.getAttribute("title") == title)
          a.disabled = false;
      }
    }
  }
}

function getActiveStyleSheet() {

  var i, a;
  for (i=0; (a = document.getElementsByTagName("link")[i]); i++) {
    if (a.getAttribute("rel").indexOf("style") != -1 &&
        a.getAttribute("title") && !a.disabled)
      return a.getAttribute("title");
  }
  return null;
}

function getPreferredStyleSheet() {

  var i, a;
  for (i=0; (a = document.getElementsByTagName("link")[i]); i++) {
    if (a.getAttribute("rel").indexOf("style") != -1 &&
        a.getAttribute("rel").indexOf("alt") == -1 &&
        a.getAttribute("title"))
      return a.getAttribute("title");
  }
  return null;
}

function createCookie(name, value, days) {

  var expires; 
  if (days) {
    var date = new Date();
    date.setTime(date.getTime() + (days*24*60*60*1000));
    expires = "; expires="+date.toGMTString();
  }
  else
    expires = "";
  document.cookie = name+"="+value+expires+"; domain=bluesnews.com; path=/";
}

function readCookie(name) {

  var nameEQ = name + "=";
  var ca = document.cookie.split(';');
  for (var i=0; i < ca.length; i++) {
    var c = ca[i];
    while (c.charAt(0) == ' ')
      c = c.substring(1, c.length);
    if (c.indexOf(nameEQ) == 0)
      return c.substring(nameEQ.length, c.length);
  }
  return null;
}

window.onload = function(e) {

  var cookie = readCookie("style");
  var title = cookie ? cookie : getPreferredStyleSheet();
  setActiveStyleSheet(title);
}

window.onunload = function(e) {

  var title = getActiveStyleSheet();
  createCookie("style", title, 365);
}

function DOMok() {

  var bGTG;
  if (document.getElementById) {
    bGTG = true;
  } else {
    bGTG = false;
  }
  return bGTG;
}

if (DOMok() == true) {
  var cookie = readCookie("style");
  var title = cookie ? cookie : getPreferredStyleSheet();
  setActiveStyleSheet(title);
}

              // Print form to set bring focus/new window cookie
              // (c)2001 James "furn" Furness <furn@base6.com>

              function SetCookie (name, value, days) {
                  // set expiry date to 'days' from now.
                  var expires = new Date();
                  expires.setTime(expires.getTime() + (days * 24 * 3600 * 1000));

                  document.cookie = name + "=" + escape(value) +
                                    "; expires=" + expires.toGMTString() +
                                    "; domain=bluesnews.com; path=/";
              }

              function GetCookie (name) {
                  var arg = name + "=";
                  var alen = arg.length;
                  var clen = document.cookie.length;
                  var i = 0;

                  while (i < clen) {
                      var j = i + alen;

                      if (document.cookie.substring(i, j) == arg)
                          return getCookieVal(j);

                      i = document.cookie.indexOf(" ", i) + 1;
                      if (i == 0)
                          break;
                  }

                  return null;
              }

              function updateTargetCookieT (obj) {
                  if (obj.checked) {
                      SetCookie("settarget", "true", 365);
                  } else {
                      SetCookie("settarget", "false", 365);
                  }
                  location.reload();
              }

              var settarget = GetCookie("settarget");

              document.write('<FORM><INPUT TYPE="checkbox" onClick="updateTargetCookieT(this)"' + (settarget == "true" ? ' CHECKED' : '') + '> Launch Links<' + '/FORM>');

      <table cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" border="0"><tr valign="bottom"><td><h2 class="posting"><a href="/s/132041/ridge-racer-unbounded-demo" target="_self">Ridge Racer Unbounded Demo</a></h2></td><td><h2 class="postdate">  [10:11 am ET] - <a href="/s/132041/ridge-racer-unbounded-demo" target="_self">Share</a> - <a href="/cgi-bin/board.pl?action=viewthread&amp;boardid=1&amp;threadid=132041" target="_self">13 Comments</a></h2></td></tr></table>
      <div class="posting">
The <a href="http://store.steampowered.com/app/202310/"><b>Ridge Racer Unbounded</b> Page on Steam</a> now offers a playable demo for the latest installment in the Ridge Racer series of racing simulations. We have no details on the demo itself, but here's a brief overview of the game: &quot;RIDGE RACER Unbounded brings an unexpected dimension to the series, delivering an original blast of ferocious racing adrenaline. Join the Unbounded street racing gang, lead by Kara Shindo, and test your driving skills against rivals in every street and alley of Shatter Bay. Prove your worth, get respect and expand your turf.&quot; Thanks Frans.
      <p></p>
      </div>      <table cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" border="0"><tr valign="bottom"><td><h2 class="posting"><a href="/s/132040/last-stronghold-3-patch-next-week" target="_self">Last Stronghold 3 Patch Next Week</a></h2></td><td><h2 class="postdate">  [10:08 am ET] - <a href="/s/132040/last-stronghold-3-patch-next-week" target="_self">Share</a> - <a href="/cgi-bin/board.pl?action=viewthread&amp;boardid=1&amp;threadid=132040" target="_self">6 Comments</a></h2></td></tr></table>
      <div class="posting">
Firefly Studios announces plans to release a new patch for <b>Stronghold 3</b> a week from today, saying the version 1.10 patch is their last planned update for the strategy sequel. Then new version will include a bunch of user-requested changes and a new &quot;Coronation&quot; multiplayer mode. Here's word: <blockquote><p><font face="Arial, Helvetica" size="2" color="#FFFF80">In Coronation Mode players will race to become the King of Kings. Players start off at the lowly rank of “Village Idiot” with limited access to buildings and military units. By generating honour players can move up the ranks, gaining new technology and weaponry along the way. For the first time in a Stronghold game Coronation mode also features upgradable keeps, which have their own defences and provide additional housing for workers and troops. The first King to achieve the rank of “Emperor” will win the game and can rightly claim to be the ultimate Stronghold Lord.<br>
</font></p></blockquote> <i><a target="_self" href="/s/132040/last-stronghold-3-patch-next-week">Continue here</a> to read the full story</i>.
      <p></p>
      </div>      <table cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" border="0"><tr valign="bottom"><td><h2 class="posting"><a href="/s/132039/blood-bowl-chaos-edition-announced" target="_self">Blood Bowl: Chaos Edition Announced</a></h2></td><td><h2 class="postdate">  [09:58 am ET] - <a href="/s/132039/blood-bowl-chaos-edition-announced" target="_self">Share</a> - <a href="/cgi-bin/board.pl?action=viewthread&amp;boardid=1&amp;threadid=132039" target="_self">14 Comments</a></h2></td></tr></table>
      <div class="posting">
The <a href="http://www.bloodbowl-game.com/index.php?rub=news-info&id=300">Blood Bowl Website</a> announces <b>Blood Bowl: Chaos Edition</b>, an updated edition of their Warhammer meets tackle football mash-up expected this September. The new edition will add three new races, a new stadium, and a new World Championship mode, though it's not stated if this is an expansion or a new product, but as we wait for more details, they offer some screenshots in the meantime, and here's a bit on what's new: &quot;World Championship mode expands even further the solo experience of Blood Bowl. From national qualifying games to continental cups to the final tournament, the competition just got bloodier! The online mode will of course be available with its intense matches, vicious private leagues, and global rankings! Get ready for another round of high fantasy football as Blood Bowl: Chaos Edition races for the touchdown!&quot;

      <table cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" border="0"><tr valign="bottom"><td><h2 class="posting"><a href="/s/132029/saints-row-3-standalone-expansion-plans" target="_self">Saints Row 3 Standalone Expansion Plans</a></h2></td><td><h2 class="postdate">  [8:24 pm ET] - <a href="/s/132029/saints-row-3-standalone-expansion-plans" target="_self">Share</a> - <a href="/cgi-bin/board.pl?action=viewthread&amp;boardid=1&amp;threadid=132029" target="_self">33 Comments</a></h2></td></tr></table>
      <div class="posting">
<a href="http://www.thq.com/uk/sr3-enter-the-dominatrix/go/article/view/homepage_article/257951/saints_row®:_the_third™_–_enter_the_dominatrix™_announced">THQ announces</a> Saints Row The Third: Enter The Dominatrix, a standalone expansion coming this fall for Volition's open world action sequel. Saying this is &quot;no longer an April Fool's dream,&quot; they promise &quot;the most requested gameplay features from the Saints Row community: freaking super powers.&quot; Here's a bit:<blockquote><p><font face="Arial, Helvetica" size="2" color="#FFFF80">Enter the Dominatrix picks up immediately following the events of Saints Row: The Third. For centuries, alien warlord Zinyak has eyed Earth and its precious natural resources and females with a watchful eye. As he prepares an armada for invasion, he has only one worry: the Third Street Saints.<br>
<br>
Once a simple street gang from Stilwater, the Saints have evolved into a global empire, replete with bombastic TV advertising and tasteful consumer products, the kind of TV advertising and consumer products that would give any alien warlord pause. Clearly, the Saints are the biggest badasses on Earth.<br>
<br>
Now, in order to prepare his forces for domination, Zinyak captures the leader of the Saints and imprisons him in an elaborate virtual reality simulation. This simulation program looks and feels like Steelport, but it is the world that has been pulled over your eyes to blind you from the truth. Here, you are a slave. Welcome... to the Dominatrix.<br>
<br>
More details and a first look at Saints Row: The Third – Enter the Dominatrix will be available this summer. Make sure you're following Saints Row on <a href="http://www.twitter.com/saintsrow">Twitter</a> and <a href="http://www.facebook.com/saintsrow">Facebook</a> to stay up to date with the latest.</font></p></blockquote>
      <p></p>
      </div>      <table cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" border="0"><tr valign="bottom"><td><h2 class="posting"><a href="/s/132028/official-the-elder-scrolls-online-announcement" target="_self">Official The Elder Scrolls Online Announcement</a></h2></td><td><h2 class="postdate">  [8:24 pm ET] - <a href="/s/132028/official-the-elder-scrolls-online-announcement" target="_self">Share</a> - <a href="/cgi-bin/board.pl?action=viewthread&amp;boardid=1&amp;threadid=132028" target="_self">42 Comments</a></h2></td></tr></table>
      <div class="posting">
<a href="http://www.marketwatch.com/story/bethesda-softworks-announces-the-elder-scrolls-online-2012-05-03">This press release</a> officially announces <b>The Elder Scrolls Online</b>, the <a target="_self" href="/s/132013/the-elder-scrolls-online-next-year">just-revealed</a> MMOG. The announcement offers a bit more on the game:<blockquote><p><font face="Arial, Helvetica" size="2" color="#FFFF80">Bethesda Softworks®, a ZeniMax® Media company, today announced The Elder Scrolls® Online, an MMO in development at ZeniMax Online Studios. The Elder Scrolls Online will be the first Elder Scrolls game to allow gamers to explore the legendary Elder Scrolls world with others.<br>
<br>
The Elder Scrolls Online is being developed for PC and Mac under the leadership of industry veteran Matt Firor, who has spent the last two decades working in online game development. Details about the game are revealed in an exclusive cover story in Game Informer®'s June issue, which ships to subscribers and newsstands this month.<br>
<br>
&quot;We have been working hard to create an online world in which players will be able to experience the epic Elder Scrolls universe with their friends, something fans have long said they wanted,&quot; said Matt Firor, game director of The Elder Scrolls Online. &quot;It will be extremely rewarding finally to unveil what we have been developing the last several years. The entire team is committed to creating the best MMO ever made - and one that is worthy of The Elder Scrolls franchise.&quot;</font></p></blockquote>
      <p></p>
      </div>      <table cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" border="0"><tr valign="bottom"><td><h2 class="posting"><a href="/s/132027/sanctum-collection-free-weekend-free-dlc" target="_self">Sanctum Collection; Free Weekend; Free DLC</a></h2></td><td><h2 class="postdate">  [8:23 pm ET] - <a href="/s/132027/sanctum-collection-free-weekend-free-dlc" target="_self">Share</a> - <a href="/cgi-bin/board.pl?action=viewthread&amp;boardid=1&amp;threadid=132027" target="_self">Post a Comment</a></h2></td></tr></table>
      <div class="posting">
Coffee Stain Studios announces the <b>Sanctum Collection</b>, a bundle that includes all the DLC for the shooter/tower defense hybrid along with the game itself. Both the <a href="http://store.steampowered.com/sub/12184/">Collection</a> and the original <a href="http://store.steampowered.com/app/91600/">Sanctum</a> are on sale on Steam for 75% off, and the game <a href="http://store.steampowered.com/news/7889/">can be played for free this weekend</a> on <a href="http://www.steampowered.com/">Steam</a>. If all that's not enough, there is also a new <a href="http://store.steampowered.com/app/91609/">free Yogscave DLC on Steam</a> as well as a <a href="http://store.steampowered.com/news/7882/">new automatic patch for the game</a>. Here are the highlights of the new version:</p>
<ul>
	<li>Brand New Medal System</li>
	<li>Improved Balancing</li>
	<li>Graphic Details Settings</li>
	<li>Under the Hood Tweaks</li>
</ul>

      </div>      <table cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" border="0"><tr valign="bottom"><td><h2 class="posting"><a href="/s/132026/the-may-hurray-bundle" target="_self">The May Hurray Bundle</a></h2></td><td><h2 class="postdate">  [8:23 pm ET] - <a href="/s/132026/the-may-hurray-bundle" target="_self">Share</a> - <a href="/cgi-bin/board.pl?action=viewthread&amp;boardid=1&amp;threadid=132026" target="_self">8 Comments</a></h2></td></tr></table>
      <div class="posting">
The <a href="http://www.indieroyale.com/">Indie Royale Website</a> now offers The May Hurray Bundle an new collection of five independent games offered at a &quot;bargain, fluctuating price.&quot; This includes <b>Dungeon Defenders</b>, <b>Containment: The Zombie Puzzler</b>, <b>Data Jammers: FastForward</b>, <b>Brainpipe - A Plunge to Unhumanity</b>, and <b>Weird Worlds: Return to Infinite Space</b>. Those who pay the equivalent of USD $7:00 or more will also receive the chiptune album <i>Future, Toward the Edge of Forever</i> by Starscream.

      </div>      <table cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" border="0"><tr valign="bottom"><td><h2 class="posting"><a href="/s/132025/mass-effect-3-connection-issues" target="_self">Mass Effect 3 Connection Issues</a></h2></td><td><h2 class="postdate">  [8:23 pm ET] - <a href="/s/132025/mass-effect-3-connection-issues" target="_self">Share</a> - <a href="/cgi-bin/board.pl?action=viewthread&amp;boardid=1&amp;threadid=132025" target="_self">17 Comments</a></h2></td></tr></table>
      <div class="posting">
<a href="http://social.bioware.com/forum/1/topic/344/index/11821829">This post</a> and <a href="http://social.bioware.com/forum/1/topic/343/index/11828744/1">this one</a> on the BioWare Social Network have complaints from players encountering errors when attempting to play <b>Mass Effect 3</b> multiplayer. Most of this seems to involve being told they require an &quot;online pass,&quot; which does not exist for the PC version of the game, as it is used as a way of combating used console game sales. There are also indications that those who own the From Ashes DLC are not even able to play the game in singleplayer mode. There are posts from players claiming they've been told BioWare is working on the problem. Thanks Mark.

      <div class="posting">
<a href="http://www.gameinformer.com/b/features/archive/2012/05/03/june-cover-revealed-the-elder-scrolls-online.aspx">Game Informer's June 2012 Cover Reveal</a> shows the next issue of the magazine will offer the official unveiling of <b>The Elder Scrolls Online</b>, finally fulfilling long-time speculation that Bethesda would one day create an MMO based on their popular RPG series. They say the game will come to Windows and OS X next year, and that a teaser trailer a screenshot will be posted tomorrow. Here's what they reveal so far:<blockquote><p><font face="Arial, Helvetica" size="2" color="#FFFF80">Developed by the team at Zenimax Online Studios, The Elder Scrolls Online merges the unmatched exploration of rich worlds that the franchise is known for with the scale and social aspects of a massively multiplayer online role-playing game. Players will discover an entirely new chapter of Elder Scrolls history in this ambitious world, set a millennium before the events of Skyrim as the daedric prince Molag Bal tries to pull all of Tamriel into his demonic realm.<br>
<br>
&quot;It will be extremely rewarding finally to unveil what we have been developing the last several years,&quot; said game director and MMO veteran Matt Firor, whose previous work includes Mythic's well-received Dark Age of Camelot. &quot;The entire team is committed to creating the best MMO ever made – and one that is worthy of The Elder Scrolls franchise.&quot;<br>
<br>
An in-depth look at everything from solo questing to public dungeons awaits in our enormous June cover story – as well as a peek at the player-driven PvP conflict that pits the three player factions against each other in open-world warfare over the province of Cyrodiil and the Emperor's throne itself.</font></p></blockquote>

      </div>      <table cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" border="0"><tr valign="bottom"><td><h2 class="posting"><a href="/s/131996/out-of-the-blue" target="_self">Out of the Blue</a></h2></td><td><h2 class="postdate">  [09:36 am ET] - <a href="/s/131996/out-of-the-blue" target="_self">Share</a> - <a href="/cgi-bin/board.pl?action=viewthread&amp;boardid=1&amp;threadid=131996" target="_self">16 Comments</a></h2></td></tr></table>
      <div class="posting">
I assume the rain overnight around here was accompanied by lightning and thunder. I didn't hear anything, but Hudson the wonder dog woke me up having one of her panic attacks that are triggered by such noises. I did my best to comfort her, and looked at the situation as another argument in favor of MrsBlue and I accepting the offer to relocate to L.A., as they rarely suffer the kind of storms that have become the norm all summer in these parts, and I'm pretty convinced her getting so freaked out by such things is shortening her lifespan.</p>
